# <a name="excel-javascript-api-requirement-sets"></a><span data-ttu-id="18ece-101">Excel JavaScript API 要求集</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-101">Excel JavaScript API requirement sets</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="18ece-102">要求集是指各组已命名的 API 成员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-102">Requirement sets are named groups of API members.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="18ece-103">Office 加载项使用清单中指定要求集，或使用运行时检查以确定是否的 Office 主机支持外接程序需要的 Api。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-103">Office Add-ins use requirement sets specified in the manifest or use a runtime check to determine whether an Office host supports APIs that an add-in needs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="18ece-104">有关详细信息，请参阅[Office 版本和要求集](https://docs.microsoft.com/office/dev/add-ins/develop/office-versions-and-requirement-sets)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-104">For more information, see [Office versions and requirement sets](https://docs.microsoft.com/office/dev/add-ins/develop/office-versions-and-requirement-sets).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="18ece-105">跨多个版本的 Office，包括 Windows、 ipad 版的 Office、 Office for Mac，和 Office Online 的 Office 2016 运行 Excel 加载项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-105">Excel add-ins run across multiple versions of Office, including Office 2016 for Windows, Office for iPad, Office for Mac, and Office Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="18ece-106">下表列出了 Excel 要求集，支持每个要求集和生成版本或数字这些应用程序的 Office 主机应用程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-106">The following table lists the Excel requirement sets, the Office host applications that support each requirement set, and the build versions or number for those applications.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="18ece-107">标记为**Beta**任何 API 不为最终用户生产做好准备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-107">Any API that is marked as **Beta** is not ready for end-user production.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="18ece-108">我们使其可供开发人员执行试用测试和开发环境中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-108">We make them available for developers to try them out in test and development environments.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="18ece-109">它们不旨在用于针对生产/业务关键文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-109">They are not meant to be used against production/business critical documents.</span></span>
> 
> <span data-ttu-id="18ece-110">对于要求集标记为**Beta**，使用指定 （或更高版本） 版的 Office 软件和使用 CDN Beta 库： https://appsforoffice.microsoft.com/lib/beta/hosted/office.js。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-110">For the requirement sets that are marked as **Beta**, use the specified (or later) version of the Office software and use the Beta library on the CDN: https://appsforoffice.microsoft.com/lib/beta/hosted/office.js.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="18ece-111">未标记为**Beta**的条目是否通常可用，以及您可以使用生产库上 CDN: https://appsforoffice.microsoft.com/lib/1/hosted/office.js。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-111">Entries not marked as **Beta** are generally available and you can use Production library on the CDN: https://appsforoffice.microsoft.com/lib/1/hosted/office.js.</span></span>

## <a name="whats-new-in-excel-javascript-api-17"></a><span data-ttu-id="18ece-167">What's new in Excel JavaScript API 1.7</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-167">What's new in Excel JavaScript API 1.7</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="18ece-168">Excel 的 JavaScript API 要求集 1.7 功能包括图表、 事件、 数据验证、 工作表、 区域、 文档属性，为项目、 保护选项和样式的 Api。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-168">The Excel JavaScript API requirement set 1.7 features include APIs for charts, events, data validation, worksheets, ranges, document properties, named items, protection options and styles.</span></span>

### <a name="customize-charts"></a><span data-ttu-id="18ece-169">自定义图表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-169">Customize charts</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="18ece-170">与新图表 Api，您可以创建其他图表类型、 向图表中添加一个数据系列，设置图表标题、 添加坐标轴标题、 添加显示单位、 添加与移动平均趋势线、 更改为线性趋势线和更多内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-170">With the new chart APIs, you can create additional chart types, add a data series to a chart, set the chart title, add an axis title, add display unit, add a trendline with moving average, change a trendline to linear, and more.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="18ece-171">以下是一些示例：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-171">The following are some examples:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-172">图表轴-获取、 设置、 格式和图表中删除轴单位、 标签和标题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-172">Chart axis - get, set, format and remove axis unit, label and title in a chart.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-173">图表系列-添加、 设置和删除图表中的一系列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-173">Chart series - add, set, and delete a series in a chart.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="18ece-174">更改系列标记、 绘图订单和大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-174">Change series markers, plot orders and sizing.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-175">图表趋势线-添加、 获取和设置图表中的趋势线的格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-175">Chart trendlines - add, get, and format trendlines in a chart.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-176">图表图例-图表中的图例字体格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-176">Chart legend - format the legend font in a chart.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-177">图表点-设置图表点颜色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-177">Chart point - set chart point color.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-178">图表标题的子字符串-获取和设置图表标题子字符串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-178">Chart title substring -  get and set title substring for a chart.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-179">图表类型-创建更多的图表类型的选项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-179">Chart type - option to create more chart types.</span></span>

### <a name="events"></a><span data-ttu-id="18ece-180">事件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-180">Events</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="18ece-181">Api 提供允许加载项以自动运行指定的函数时特定事件的事件处理程序的各种 Excel 事件发生。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-181">Excel events APIs provide a variety of event handlers that allow your add-in to automatically run a designated function when a specific event occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="18ece-182">可以将函数设计为执行方案所需的任何操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-182">You can design that function to perform whatever actions your scenario requires.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="18ece-183">当前可用的事件的列表，请参阅[使用使用 Excel JavaScript API 的事件](https://docs.microsoft.com/office/dev/add-ins/excel/excel-add-ins-events)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-183">For a list of events that are currently available, see [Work with Events using the Excel JavaScript API](https://docs.microsoft.com/office/dev/add-ins/excel/excel-add-ins-events).</span></span>

### <a name="customize-the-appearance-of-worksheets-and-ranges"></a><span data-ttu-id="18ece-184">自定义工作表和区域的外观</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-184">Customize the appearance of worksheets and ranges</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="18ece-185">使用新的 Api，您可以自定义工作表以多种方式的外观：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-185">Using the new APIs, you can customize the appearance of worksheets in multiple ways:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-186">冻结窗格保留特定的行或列可见滚动工作表中时。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-186">Freeze panes to keep specific rows or columns visible when you scroll in the worksheet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="18ece-187">例如，如果在工作表中的第一行包含标头，您可能冻结该行，以便向工作表下滚动，仍可见列标题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-187">For example, if the first row in your worksheet contains headers, you might freeze that row so that the column headers will remain visible as you scroll down the worksheet.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-188">修改工作表标签颜色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-188">Modify the worksheet tab color.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-189">添加表的标题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-189">Add worksheet headings.</span></span>


<span data-ttu-id="18ece-190">您可以自定义区域以多种方式的外观：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-190">You can customize the appearance of ranges in multiple ways:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-191">设置以确保范围的单元格样式确保范围中的所有单元格具有一致的格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-191">Set the cell style for a range to ensure sure that all cells in the range have consistent formatting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="18ece-192">单元格样式是一组定义的格式特征，如字体和字体大小、 数字格式、 单元格边框和单元格底纹。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-192">A cell style is a defined set of formatting characteristics, such as fonts and font sizes, number formats, cell borders, and cell shading.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="18ece-193">可以使用任何 Excel 的内置单元格样式或创建您自己的自定义的单元格样式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-193">Use any of Excel's built-in cell styles or create your own custom cell style.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-194">设置范围内的文本方向。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-194">Set the text orientation for a range.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-195">添加或修改区域链接到工作簿中的另一个位置或外部位置上的超链接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-195">Add or modify a hyperlink on a range that links to another location in the workbook or to an external location.</span></span>

### <a name="manage-document-properties"></a><span data-ttu-id="18ece-196">管理文档属性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-196">Manage document properties</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="18ece-197">使用 Api 中的文档属性，您可以访问内置文档属性和还创建和管理自定义文档属性，用于存储工作簿和驱动器的工作流和业务逻辑的状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-197">Using the document properties APIs, you can access built-in document properties and also create and manage custom document properties to store state of the workbook and drive workflow and business logic.</span></span>

### <a name="copy-worksheets"></a><span data-ttu-id="18ece-198">复制工作表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-198">Copy worksheets</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="18ece-199">使用工作表复制 Api，可以将从一个工作表的数据和格式复制到同一工作簿中的新工作表并减少所需的数据传输的量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-199">Using the worksheet copy APIs, you can copy the data and format from one worksheet to a new worksheet within the same workbook and reduce the amount of data transfer needed.</span></span>

### <a name="handle-ranges-with-ease"></a><span data-ttu-id="18ece-200">轻松地处理范围</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-200">Handle ranges with ease</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="18ece-201">使用各种范围 Api，您可以执行诸如 get 周围的区域，获取调整大小的范围和详细信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-201">Using the various range APIs, you can do things such as get the surrounding region, get a resized range, and more.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="18ece-202">这些 Api 应使任务，如范围操作和解决更加有效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-202">These APIs should make tasks like range manipulation and addressing much more efficient.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="18ece-203">此外：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-203">In addition:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-204">工作簿和工作表的保护选项-使用这些 Api 来保护工作表和工作簿结构中的数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-204">Workbook and worksheet protection options - use these APIs to protect data in a worksheet and the workbook structure.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-205">更新已命名的项目-使用此 API 更新已命名的项目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-205">Update a named item - use this API to update a named item.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-206">获取活动单元格-使用此 API 获取工作簿的活动单元格。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-206">Get active cell  - use this API to get the active cell of a workbook.</span></span>

## <a name="whats-new-in-excel-javascript-api-16"></a><span data-ttu-id="18ece-1279">What's new in Excel JavaScript API 1.6</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1279">What's new in Excel JavaScript API 1.6</span></span> 

### <a name="conditional-formatting"></a><span data-ttu-id="18ece-1280">条件格式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1280">Conditional formatting</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="18ece-1281">介绍区域的条件格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1281">Introduces conditional formating of a range.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="18ece-1282">允许以下类型的条件格式：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1282">Allows the following types of conditional formatting:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-1283">彩色温标</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1283">Color scale</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-1284">数据栏</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1284">Data bar</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-1285">图标集</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1285">Icon set</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-1286">自定义</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1286">Custom</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="18ece-1287">此外：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1287">In addition:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-1288">返回条件格式应用于的区域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1288">Returns the range the conditional format is applied to.</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-1289">条件格式的删除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1289">Removal of conditional formatting.</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-1290">提供了优先级和 stopifTrue 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1290">Provides priority and stopifTrue capability.</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-1291">获取给定范围内所有条件格式的集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1291">Get collection of all conditional formatting on a given range.</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-1292">清除当前指定范围中处于活动状态的所有条件格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1292">Clears all conditional formats active on the current specified range.</span></span>

##  <a name="whats-new-in-excel-javascript-api-15"></a><span data-ttu-id="18ece-1812">What's new in Excel JavaScript API 1.5</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1812">What's new in Excel JavaScript API 1.5</span></span>

### <a name="custom-xml-part"></a><span data-ttu-id="18ece-1813">自定义 XML 部件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1813">Custom XML part</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-1814">将自定义 XML 部件集合添加到工作簿对象中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1814">Addition of custom XML parts collection to workbook object.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-1815">使用 ID 获取自定义 XML 部件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1815">Get custom XML part using ID</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-1816">获取其命名空间匹配给定命名空间的自定义 XML 部件的新作用域内集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1816">Get a new scoped collection of custom XML parts whose namespaces match the given namespace.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-1817">获取与某个部件关联的 XML 字符串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1817">Get XML string associated with a part.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-1818">提供部件的 ID 和命名空间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1818">Provide id and namespace of a part.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-1819">向工作簿添加新的自定义 XML 部件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1819">Adds a new custom XML part to the workbook.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-1820">设置整个 XML 部件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1820">Set entire XML part.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-1821">删除自定义 XML 部件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1821">Delete a custom XML part.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-1822">删除其给定名称来自由 xpath 标识的元素的属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1822">Delete an attribute with the given name from the element identified by xpath.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-1823">按 xpath 查询 XML 内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1823">Query the XML content by xpath.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-1824">插入、更新和删除属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1824">Insert, update and delete attribute.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="18ece-1825">**参考实现：** 请参阅[此处](https://github.com/mandren/Excel-CustomXMLPart-Demo)，了解说明如何在外接程序中使用自定义 XML 部件的参考实现。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1825">**Reference implementation:** Please refer [here](https://github.com/mandren/Excel-CustomXMLPart-Demo) for a reference implementation that shows how custom XML parts can be used in an add-in.</span></span>

### <a name="others"></a><span data-ttu-id="18ece-1826">其他</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1826">Others</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-p275">`range.getSurroundingRegion()` 返回一个 Range 对象，该对象表示此范围的周围区域。周围区域是由相对于该范围的空白行和空白列的任何组合所限定的范围。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-p275">`range.getSurroundingRegion()` Returns a Range object that represents the surrounding region for this range. A surrounding region is a range bounded by any combination of blank rows and blank columns relative to this range.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-1829">对表列执行 `getNextColumn()`、`getPreviousColumn()` 以及 \`getLast() 操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1829">`getNextColumn()` and `getPreviousColumn()`, \`getLast() on table column.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-1830">对工作簿执行 `getActiveWorksheet()` 操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1830">`getActiveWorksheet()` on the workbook.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-1831">工作簿的 `getRange(address: string)` 关闭。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1831">`getRange(address: string)` off of workbook.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-p276">`getBoundingRange(ranges: )` 获取包含提供的范围的最小 range 对象。例如，介于 “B2:C5” 和 “D10:E15” 之间的边界范围为 “B2:E15”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-p276">`getBoundingRange(ranges: )` Gets the smallest range object that encompasses the provided ranges. For example, the bounding range between "B2:C5" and "D10:E15" is "B2:E15".</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-1834">对各种集合（例如已命名项目、工作表、表等）执行 `getCount()` 操作以获取集合中的项目数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1834">`getCount()` on various collections such as named item, worksheet, table, etc. to get number of items in a collection.</span></span> `workbook.worksheets.getCount()`
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-1835">对各种集合（如工作表、表列、图标点、范围视图集合）执行 `getFirst()` 和 `getLast()` 以及 get last 操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1835">`getFirst()` and `getLast()` and get last on various collection such as tworksheet, able column, chart points, range view collection.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-1836">对工作表、表列集合执行 `getNext()` 和 `getPrevious()` 操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1836">`getNext()` and `getPrevious()` on worksheet, table column collection.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-1837">`getRangeR1C1()` 获取以特定行索引和列索引开始并跨越了一定数量的行和列的 range 对象。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1837">`getRangeR1C1()` Gets the range object beginning at a particular row index and column index, and spanning a certain number of rows and columns.</span></span>

## <a name="whats-new-in-excel-javascript-api-14"></a><span data-ttu-id="18ece-1947">Excel JavaScript API 1.4 的最近更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1947">What's new in Excel JavaScript API 1.4</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="18ece-1948">以下是新增功能要求中的 Excel JavaScript Api 设置 1.4。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1948">The following are the new additions to the Excel JavaScript APIs in requirement set 1.4.</span></span>

### <a name="named-item-add-and-new-properties"></a><span data-ttu-id="18ece-1949">添加了已命名项和新属性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1949">Named item add and new properties</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="18ece-1950">新属性：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1950">New properties:</span></span>

* `comment`
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-1951">`scope`：限定到工作表或工作簿的项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1951">`scope` worksheet or workbook scoped items</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-1952">`worksheet`：返回已命名项限定到的工作表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1952">`worksheet` returns the worksheet on which the named item is scoped to.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="18ece-1953">新方法：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1953">New methods:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-1954">`add(name: string, reference: Range or string, comment: string)`：将新名称添加到给定范围的集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1954">`add(name: string, reference: Range or string, comment: string)`Adds a new name to the collection of the given scope.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-1955">`addFormulaLocal(name: string, formula: string, comment: string)`：使用用户的公式区域设置，将新名称添加到给定范围的集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1955">`addFormulaLocal(name: string, formula: string, comment: string)` Adds a new name to the collection of the given scope using the user's locale for the formula.</span></span>

### <a name="settings-api-in-in-excel-namespace"></a><span data-ttu-id="18ece-1956">Excel 命名空间中的设置 API</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1956">Settings API in in Excel namespace</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="18ece-p286">[Setting](/javascript/api/excel/excel.setting) 对象表示文档保留设置的键值对。现在，我们已在 Excel 命名空间下添加了与设置相关的 API。这不会提供全新功能，但可便于继续使用基于承诺的批处理 API 语法，减少对 Excel 相关任务常见 API 的依赖。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-p286">[Setting](/javascript/api/excel/excel.setting) object represents a key-value pair of a setting persisted to the document. Now, we've added settings related APIs under Excel namespace. This doesn't offer net new functionality - however this make easy to remain in the promise based batched API syntax reduce the dependency on common API for Excel related tasks.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="18ece-1960">API 包括通过键获取设置条目的 `getItem()`，以及将指定键值设置对添加到工作簿的 `add()`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1960">APIs include `getItem()` to get setting entry via the key, `add()` to add the specified key:value setting pair to the workbook.</span></span>

### <a name="others"></a><span data-ttu-id="18ece-1961">其他</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1961">Others</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-1962">设置表列名称（旧版只允许读取）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1962">Set table column name (prior version only allows reading).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-1963">将表列添加到表的末尾（旧版只允许添加到除末尾之外的其他任何位置）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1963">Add table column to the end of the table (prior version only allows anywhere but last).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-1964">一次性向表中添加多行（旧版只允许一次添加 1 行）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1964">Add multiple rows to a table at a time (prior version only allows 1 row at a time).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-1965">`range.getColumnsAfter(count: number)` 和 `range.getColumnsBefore(count: number)` 分别用于获取当前 Range 对象的右/左侧的一定数量的列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-1965">`range.getColumnsAfter(count: number)` and `range.getColumnsBefore(count: number)` to get a certain number of columns to the right/left of the current Range object.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="18ece-p287">获取项或 NULL 对象函数：此功能允许使用键获取对象。如果没有对象，返回的对象的 isNullObject 属性为 true。这样一来，开发者可以检查对象是否存在，而无需通过异常处理来进行处理。适用于工作表、已命名项、绑定、图表系列等</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-p287">Get item or null object function: This functionality allows getting object using a key. If the object does not exist, the returned object's isNullObject property will be true. This alows developers to check if an object exists or not without having to handle it thorugh exception handling. Available on worksheet, named-item, binding, chart series, etc.</span></span>

    ```javascript
    worksheet.GetItemOrNullObject()
    ```

## <a name="excel-javascript-api-11"></a><span data-ttu-id="18ece-2742">Excel JavaScript API 1.1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="18ece-2742">Excel JavaScript API 1.1</span></span>
